CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Vs Plan $]
 AS [Measures].[Actual]-[Measures].[YTD Plan], 
FORMAT_STRING = "$#,##0.00;($#,##0.00)", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Fact GL';    
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Plan vs PY Proj %]
 AS iif([Measures].[PYTD Projected]=0,0,([Measures].[Plan]-[Measures].[PYTD Projected])/[Measures].[PYTD Projected]), 
FORMAT_STRING = "Percent",

 AS [Measures].[Plan]-[Measures].[PYTD Projected],

              <xs:schema id="Prelude_x0020_ODS" xmlns="" xmlns:xs="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema" xmlns:msdata="urn:schemas-microsoft-com:xml-msdata" xmlns:msprop="urn:schemas-microsoft-com:xml-msprop">

                  <xs:complexType>
                    <xs:choice minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded">
                      <xs:element name="dbo_pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods" msprop:IsLogical="True" msprop:FriendlyName="FactGL" msprop:DbTableName="FactGL" msprop:TableType="View" msprop:QueryDefinition="SELECT     dbo.pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods.CompanyID, dbo.pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods.DivisionNum, dbo.pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods.LocationNum, &#xD;&#xA;                      dbo.pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods.CostCenterNum, dbo.pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods.AccountNum, dbo.pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods.Vmc, &#xD;&#xA;                      dbo.pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods.Period, dbo.pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods.Debits, dbo.pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods.Credits, &#xD;&#xA;                      dbo.pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods.Budget1 AS [Plan], dbo.pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods.Budget2, dbo.pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods.Budget3, &#xD;&#xA;                      dbo.pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods.Budget4, dbo.pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods.SourceSystemPrimaryKey, dbo.pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods.ExportDate, &#xD;&#xA;                      CASE WHEN RIGHT(CONVERT(VARCHAR(7), GETDATE(), 120), 5) &lt;= pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods.Period THEN 0 ELSE Debits - Credits END AS Actual, &#xD;&#xA;                      CASE WHEN RIGHT(CONVERT(VARCHAR(7), GETDATE(), 120), 5) &lt;= pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods.Period THEN 0 ELSE 1 END AS PeriodComplete, &#xD;&#xA;                      dbo.pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods.DivisionNum + dbo.pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods.LocationNum + dbo.pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods.CostCenterNum + dbo.pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods.AccountNum&#xD;&#xA;                       AS PrefixPlusAccount, CASE WHEN RIGHT(CONVERT(VARCHAR(7), GETDATE(), 120), 5) &#xD;&#xA;                      &lt;= pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods.Period THEN 0 ELSE PYTActual END AS PYTActual, CASE WHEN RIGHT(CONVERT(VARCHAR(7), GETDATE(), 120), 5) &#xD;&#xA;                      &lt;= pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods.Period THEN CASE WHEN (MONTH(GETDATE()) - 1) = 0 THEN 0 ELSE SumPeriod.SumActual / (MONTH(GETDATE()) - 1) &#xD;&#xA;                      END ELSE Debits - Credits END AS RunRate, SumPeriod.SumActual, SumPeriod.SumPlan, CASE WHEN RIGHT(CONVERT(VARCHAR(7), GETDATE(), 120), 5) &#xD;&#xA;                            GROUP BY CP_1.CompanyID, CP_1.DivisionNum, CP_1.LocationNum, CP_1.CostCenterNum, CP_1.AccountNum, CP_1.Period) AS SumPeriod ON &#xD;&#xA;                      dbo.pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods.Period = SumPeriod.Period AND dbo.pChartOfAccountsStatPeriods.AccountNum = SumPeriod.AccountNum AND &#xD;&#xA;
